CELEBRITY ADDRESSES MEGA LIST-- 
Tons And Tons of Celebrities Home Addresses!!!

Normally there would be privacy conerns if these were private
individuals but because these are notable people and the fact that the
addresses provided are already published and well known to the general
public, they are a matter of public information.

mAnAmAnAhAs
 
You will notice a few celebrity 'entities' like music 'bands' in this 
list as well,but most of them, as you can see, are individual 
celebrities. Inaddition, there may be a few defunct entities or deceased 
celebrities mentioned here too. 
The reason for this is because, even though celebrities die or go out 
of business, their families or business associates often maintain some 
contact with the public because of the continued public interest in their 
work. The list is far too extensive to edit out the dead and defunct.
 
The addresses shown are agents, fan addresses or home addresses where
celebrities are known to receive mail. At the bottom I have added some
additional links that may help you find even more addresses than those
mentioned here.
 
Brace yourself - the is enormous!

In the celebrity address circle, updated lists contain NEW addresses
but very rarely edit out old ones. The reason, as I mentioned above,
is because agents, companies and family members often remain in
contact with the public because of contuing public interest in the
defunct celebrity's work. Bob Hope's wife Delores, for example, who I
have contacted on more than one occassion in the past, continued for
quite some time to manage Bob's fan mail because he had signed
literally thousands of photographs before his death and she continued
to distribute them to whomever asked for them.
 
Hope Bob 10346 Moorpark Street North Hollywood, CA 91602
Hope Bob 3808 W. Riverside Drive Burbank, CA 91505
 
So you see, the fact that there are multiple addresses or the fact
that a celebrity is no longer with us or no longer in business does
not prevent a reply. Many people, like Delores (who incidentally is
somewhat of a celbrity herself)...
 
INTERNET MOVIE DATABASE
http://www.imdb.com/name/nm1052625/
 
...would probably be quite honored and flattered at your recognition
of Bob's birthday or other achievements. Furthermore, if you take a
closer look at the list I provided, this is not a run-of-the-mill
list. In some instances the address listed is the actual STREET
ADDRESS for that celebrity - where he or she actually takes out the
trash - as opposed to some agent who may or may never pass the letter
on. In fact, there are over a hundred HOME ADDRESSES listed on this
link alone:
 
HOLLYWOOD
http://www.hollywoodusa.co.uk/celebrity-homes.htm
Celebrity & Movie Stars Street Addresses in Hollywood and Los Angeles.
 
Normally there would be privacy conerns if these were private
individuals but because these are notable people and the fact that the
addresses provided are already published and well known to the general
public, they are a matter of public information. Again, because these
lists are generally not edited to remove those who are defunct for the
reasons I mentioned, the list simply grows. A determined fan must weed
through them and choose his contacts carefully.
